[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  20 +[38;2;248;248;242m## What I Did                                                                                                                                                             [49m[39m

[5C[38;2;220;90;90m[48;2;61;1;0m  27 -[38;2;248;248;242m- `.env`                                                                                                                                                                  [49m[39m

[5C[38;2;220;90;90m[48;2;61;1;0m  30 -[38;2;248;248;242m  Service name, endpoint, response format, and default parameters.                                                                                                        [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;220;90;90m[48;2;61;1;0m  31 -[38;2;248;248;242m- `api_client.py`                                                                                                                                                         [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;220;90;90m[48;2;61;1;0m  32 -[38;2;248;248;242m  Shared API client that loads config, calls a named service, parses XML/JSON, and can store results in PostgreSQL.                                                       [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;220;90;90m[48;2;61;1;0m  33 -[38;2;248;248;242m- `traffic_info_api_client.py`, `acc_info_api_client.py`                                                                                                                  [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;220;90;90m[48;2;61;1;0m  34 -[38;2;248;248;242m  Service-specific clients built on top of the shared layer.                                                                                                              [49m[39m

[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  46 +[38;2;248;248;242m- **Error localisation (H0):** Olympic Expressway (link 1150006000/6500) had the worst ETA overrun at **+352%** during the 7–9 AM peak. The worst links all cluster on art[49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m     +[38;2;248;248;242merial corridors entering the city centre.                                                                                                                                 [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  47 +[38;2;248;248;242m- **H1 confirmed:** Speed on the top-10 error links drops from 71.9 km/h at 06:00 to 32.6 km/h by 09:00 — a **45.5% collapse** that a mean-based ETA cannot anticipate.   [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  48 +[38;2;248;248;242m- **H2 confirmed:** The Olympic Expressway day-to-day coefficient of variation (CV) at 8 AM is **0.66** — yesterday's average is essentially useless as a point estimate. [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  49 +[38;2;248;248;242m- **H3 confirmed:** A vehicle breakdown on the Olympic Expressway was recorded in `navigation_db.acc_info_history` at **07:31, lasting 55 minutes through peak hour** — di[49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m     +[38;2;248;248;242mrectly matching the highest-error road from H0.                                                                                                                           [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  50 +[38;2;248;248;242m- **H4 confirmed:** Across all 3,611 peak-hour links, CV = 0.52 and **12.6% of link-hours exceed 30% ETA error**, proving a single mean value is structurally inadequate f[49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m     +[38;2;248;248;242mor high-variance peak conditions.                                                                                                                                         [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;248;248;242m[2m [1C51[1C[22m [39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  52 +[38;2;248;248;242m#### VOC2 — Detour Route Analysis (`voc2_analysis.py`)                                                                                                                    [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  53 +[38;2;248;248;242m                                                                                                                                                                          [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  54 +[38;2;248;248;242mTwo competing routes were constructed from real data:                                                                                                                     [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  55 +[38;2;248;248;242m                                                                                                                                                                          [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  56 +[38;2;248;248;242m| Route | Road | Distance | Characteristics |                                                                                                                             [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  57 +[38;2;248;248;242m|-------|------|----------|-----------------|                                                                                                                             [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  58 +[38;2;248;248;242m| **Route A** (direct) | Olympic Expressway | 18.5 km | Urban motorway — fast but volatile |                                                                              [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  59 +[38;2;248;248;242m| **Route B** (detour) | Dongil-ro · Cheonho-daero | 18.3 km | Arterial — slow but stable |                                                                               [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  60 +[38;2;248;248;242m                                                                                                                                                                          [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  61 +[38;2;248;248;242mRoute A is faster in every time slot under normal conditions. The question was: what causes the navigation to prefer Route B?                                             [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  62 +[38;2;248;248;242m                                                                                                                                                                          [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  63 +[38;2;248;248;242m| Hypothesis | Finding |                                                                                                                                                  [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  64 +[38;2;248;248;242m|------------|---------|                                                                                                                                                  [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  65 +[38;2;248;248;242m| **H1** — Speed over-estimation | Route A must be underestimated by **≥33%** for Route B to win on cost. This actually happened on **10 of 31 days (32%)** in March — on [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m     +[38;2;248;248;242mthose days, the detour was justified. |                                                                                                                                   [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  66 +[38;2;248;248;242m| **H2** — Stale road restriction (**most likely root cause**) | If a closure on Route A was cleared but the navigation DB was not yet updated, the system avoids a passab[49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m     +[38;2;248;248;242mle road. The AccInfo `exp_clr_date` lag mechanism directly explains persistent detours on the other 21 days. |                                                            [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  67 +[38;2;248;248;242m| **H3** — Cost function bias | With only 0.2 km distance difference between the two routes, the distance weight β would need to be 55.52 min/km to flip the cost — unreal[49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m     +[38;2;248;248;242mistic. However, in the original 10 km vs 30 km scenario, a small β **is** enough to cause the issue. |                                                                    [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  68 +[38;2;248;248;242m| **H4** — Re-routing trigger too sensitive | Route A's 8 AM speed std dev is ±24.2 km/h. A simple speed threshold triggers re-routing during temporary congestion, lockin[49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m     +[38;2;248;248;242mg the user into Route B even after congestion clears. |                                                                                                                   [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  69 +[38;2;248;248;242m                                                                                                                                                                          [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  70 +[38;2;248;248;242m---                                                                                                                                                                       [49m[39m
[5C[38;2;80;200;80m[48;2;2;40;0m  71 +[38;2;248;248;242m                                                                                                                                                                          [49m[39m
